Assignment from a sparse matrix with the same storage order 

Convert from a sparse matrix to block sparse matrix. \begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
Before calling this function, tt is necessary to call either \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_block_sparse_matrix_acad69e4bb5e747db973cacc75c2f4a4d}{set\+Block\+Layout()} (matrices with variable-\/size blocks) or \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_block_sparse_matrix_a1984d81fa41dc2f4e8f1208f602e7e45}{set\+Block\+Size()} (for fixed-\/size blocks). 
\end{DoxyWarning}

Allocate the internal array of pointers to blocks and their inner indices 

\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
For fixed-\/size blocks, call \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_block_sparse_matrix_a1984d81fa41dc2f4e8f1208f602e7e45}{set\+Block\+Size()} to set the block. And For variable-\/size blocks, call \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_block_sparse_matrix_acad69e4bb5e747db973cacc75c2f4a4d}{set\+Block\+Layout()} before using this function
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em nonzerosblocks} & \doxylink{test__concurrent__vector__v2_8cpp_a36bc74cc1ee36b525959509e2a81c81e}{Number} of nonzero blocks. The total number of nonzeros is is computed in \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_block_sparse_matrix_acad69e4bb5e747db973cacc75c2f4a4d}{set\+Block\+Layout()} for variable-\/size blocks \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setBlockLayout()}{setBlockLayout()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_eigen_1_1_block_sparse_matrix_acad69e4bb5e747db973cacc75c2f4a4d} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_block_sparse_matrix}{Eigen\+::\+Block\+Sparse\+Matrix}}$<$ \+\_\+\+Scalar, \+\_\+\+Block\+At\+Compile\+Time, \+\_\+\+Options, \+\_\+\+Storage\+Index $>$\+::set\+Block\+Layout (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const Vector\+Xi \&}]{row\+Blocks}{, }\item[{const Vector\+Xi \&}]{col\+Blocks}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Set the row and column block layouts, 

This function set the size of each row and column block. So this function should be used only for blocks with variable size. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em row\+Blocks} & \+: \doxylink{test__concurrent__vector__v2_8cpp_a36bc74cc1ee36b525959509e2a81c81e}{Number} of rows per row block \\
\hline
{\em col\+Blocks} & \+: \doxylink{test__concurrent__vector__v2_8cpp_a36bc74cc1ee36b525959509e2a81c81e}{Number} of columns per column block \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

set the block size at runtime for fixed-\/size block layout 

Call this only for fixed-\/size blocks \Hypertarget{class_eigen_1_1_block_sparse_matrix_a40891e477661e68bc870319d1379c7aa}\index{Eigen::BlockSparseMatrix$<$ \_Scalar, \_BlockAtCompileTime, \_Options, \_StorageIndex $>$::BlockInnerIterator@{Eigen::BlockSparseMatrix$<$ \_Scalar, \_BlockAtCompileTime, \_Options, \_StorageIndex $>$::BlockInnerIterator}!setBlockStructure@{setBlockStructure}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setBlockStructure()}{setBlockStructure()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_eigen_1_1_block_sparse_matrix_a40891e477661e68bc870319d1379c7aa} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_block_sparse_matrix}{Eigen\+::\+Block\+Sparse\+Matrix}}$<$ \+\_\+\+Scalar, \+\_\+\+Block\+At\+Compile\+Time, \+\_\+\+Options, \+\_\+\+Storage\+Index $>$\+::set\+Block\+Structure (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_transform}{Matrix\+Type}} \&}]{block\+Pattern}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Set the nonzero block pattern of the matrix 

Given a sparse matrix describing the nonzero block pattern, this function prepares the internal pointers for values. After calling this function, any {\itshape nonzero} block (bi, bj) can be set with a simple call to coeff\+Ref(bi,bj).

\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
Before calling this function, tt is necessary to call either \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_block_sparse_matrix_acad69e4bb5e747db973cacc75c2f4a4d}{set\+Block\+Layout()} (matrices with variable-\/size blocks) or \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_block_sparse_matrix_a1984d81fa41dc2f4e8f1208f602e7e45}{set\+Block\+Size()} (for fixed-\/size blocks).
\end{DoxyWarning}

\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em block\+Pattern} & \doxylink{struct_eigen_1_1_sparse}{Sparse} matrix of boolean elements describing the block structure\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{参见}
\doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_block_sparse_matrix_acad69e4bb5e747db973cacc75c2f4a4d}{set\+Block\+Layout()} 

\doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_block_sparse_matrix_a1984d81fa41dc2f4e8f1208f602e7e45}{set\+Block\+Size()}

\Hypertarget{class_eigen_1_1_block_sparse_matrix_aa148b63f89555f4eed312638abe597eb}\index{Eigen::BlockSparseMatrix$<$ \_Scalar, \_BlockAtCompileTime, \_Options, \_StorageIndex $>$::BlockInnerIterator@{Eigen::BlockSparseMatrix$<$ \_Scalar, \_BlockAtCompileTime, \_Options, \_StorageIndex $>$::BlockInnerIterator}!setFromTriplets@{setFromTriplets}}
\index{setFromTriplets@{setFromTriplets}!Eigen::BlockSparseMatrix$<$ \_Scalar, \_BlockAtCompileTime, \_Options, \_StorageIndex $>$::BlockInnerIterator@{Eigen::BlockSparseMatrix$<$ \_Scalar, \_BlockAtCompileTime, \_Options, \_StorageIndex $>$::BlockInnerIterator}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setFromTriplets()}{setFromTriplets()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_eigen_1_1_block_sparse_matrix_aa148b63f89555f4eed312638abe597eb} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_block_sparse_matrix}{Eigen\+::\+Block\+Sparse\+Matrix}}$<$ \+\_\+\+Scalar, \+\_\+\+Block\+At\+Compile\+Time, \+\_\+\+Options, \+\_\+\+Storage\+Index $>$\+::set\+From\+Triplets (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const Input\+Iterator \&}]{begin}{, }\item[{const Input\+Iterator \&}]{end}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Fill values in a matrix from a triplet list. 

Each triplet item has a block stored in an \doxylink{namespace_eigen}{Eigen} dense matrix. The Input\+Iterator class should provide the functions \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_block_sparse_matrix_1_1_block_inner_iterator_aea32008c273aa202f17d7689e3b8bbfa}{row()}, \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_block_sparse_matrix_1_1_block_inner_iterator_abf1450340b2e595896de9dfc7660513e}{col()} and \doxylink{imgui__impl__opengl3__loader_8h_abe8e049f756b5ba547bda825af81b645}{value()}

\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
For fixed-\/size blocks, call \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_block_sparse_matrix_a1984d81fa41dc2f4e8f1208f602e7e45}{set\+Block\+Size()} before this function.
\end{DoxyNote}
